FNV PBR CLOSE TERRAIN RUNTIME LAYER/CONSTANT CONTRACT AUDIT

Goal:
- Prove close-terrain TEX_COUNT/layer ownership instead of assuming seven layers.
- Prove which land-ish variants own diffuse/normal arrays and which are projected-shadow, SI, LandO, landlo-fog, or point-light rows.
- Check whether vanilla supplies the constants NVR close-terrain shaders expect, and which constants must be uploaded by Psycho.

======================================================================
NVR CLOSE TERRAIN ABI TO PROVE AGAINST VANILLA
======================================================================
Textures: BaseMap[7] at s0..s6, NormalMap[7] at s7..s13.
Layer count: TEX_COUNT macro must match active layer count; do not assume 7 for every row.
Blend inputs: blend_0.xyzw plus blend_1.xyz feed seven layer weights.
Pixel constants: AmbientColor c1, SunColor c3, SunDir c18, LandSpec c32/c33, LandHeight c34/c35, FogParam c36, FogColor c37.
Point light variants additionally need PointLightColor c39, PointLightPosition c63, PointLightCount c88.
PBR controls: TESR_TerrainData c89 and TESR_TerrainExtraData c90 are NVR-owned extras, not vanilla constants.
Replacement is valid only if the active runtime row owns these textures/constants or has a proven fallback.

======================================================================

======================================================================
